               <div class="jeg_postblock_content">
                <h3 class="jeg_post_title" property="headline">
                 <a href="https://www.premiumtimesng.com/opinion/450424-denmark-takes-the-law-into-its-own-hands-by-dakuku-peterside.html">
                  Denmark Takes the Law Into Its Own Hands?, By Dakuku Peterside
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="jeg_post_meta">
                 <div class="jeg_meta_author coauthor">
                  <span class="meta_text by">
                   by
                  </span>
                  <a href="https://www.premiumtimesng.com/author/dakukupeterside">
                   Dakuku Peterside
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="jeg_meta_date">
                  <a href="https://www.premiumtimesng.com/opinion/450424-denmark-takes-the-law-into-its-own-hands-by-dakuku-peterside.html">
                   <i class="fa fa-clock-o">
                   </i>
                   March 22, 2021
                  </a>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="jeg_post_excerpt">
                 <p>
                  Last week, something with significant but far-reaching diplomatic implications happened in security circles, particularly in the maritime security sphere. Denmark, a tiny...
                 </p>
                 <a class="jeg_readmore" href="https://www.premiumtimesng.com/opinion/450424-denmark-takes-the-law-into-its-own-hands-by-dakuku-peterside.html">
                  Read more
                 </a>
